    }

<div class="co_section_branding hide_for_print" title="Tzivos Hashem Club">
<div class="section_title ">
<a href="/kids/article_cdo/aid/354741/jewish/Tzivos-Hashem-Club.htm">Tzivos Hashem Club</a>
</div>
</div>
<div class="clearfix bh mobile-only align_right">ב"ה</div>
<div class="master-content-wrapper g960" >
<header class="article-header cf ">
<script type="application/ld+json">

<div class="breadcrumbs breadcrumbs hide_for_print" data-list-name="breadcrumbs">
<a class="breadcrumbs__crumb" href='/kids/default_cdo/jewish/JewishKidsorg.htm' data-aid="334370">
JewishKids.org
</a>
<span class="breadcrumbs__divider fa fa-angle-end"></span>
<a class="breadcrumbs__crumb" href='/kids/article_cdo/aid/354741/jewish/Tzivos-Hashem-Club.htm' data-aid="354741">
Tzivos Hashem Club
</a>
</div>
<h1 class="article-header__title js-article-title js-page-title">About Tzivos Hashem</h1>
<div>
</div>
</header>
</div>
<div class="body_wrapper clearfix co_body">
<div class="g700" id="co_body_container">
<div id="ContentBody">
<div class="content-area-parent no_margin">
<div >
<div id="co_content_container" class="content g700 no_margin">
<article class="content js-content" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Article">
<meta itemprop="mainEntityOfPage headline name" content="About Tzivos Hashem" />
<meta itemprop="image" content="https://w2.chabad.org/media/images/852/DroV8525525.jpg" />
<meta itemprop="thumbnailUrl" content="https://w2.chabad.org/media/images/110/VDsr1106037.jpg" />
<meta itemprop="thumbnailUrl" content="https://w2.chabad.org/media/images/852/DroV8525525.jpg" />
<meta itemprop="thumbnailUrl" content="https://w2.chabad.org/media/images/68/OXYl681405.jpg" />
<meta itemprop="uploadDate" content="2006-03-01T14:58:23" />
<span itemprop="publisher" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Organization">
<meta itemprop="name" content="Chabad.org" />
<meta itemprop="brand" content="Chabad.org" />
<span itemprop="logo" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject">
<meta itemprop="url" content="https://w2.chabad.org/images/logos/chabad.org.amp.60_330.png" />
<meta itemprop="height" content="60" />
<meta itemprop="width" content="330" />
</span>
</span>
<meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2006-03-01T14:58:23" />
<div align="Right" class="imagetable right" width="159" >
<img src="https://w2.chabad.org/media/images/852/DroV8525525.jpg?_i=_nF75D98DAEBA4CF2B502564351699CD99" itemprop="image" srcset="https://w2.chabad.org/media/images/852/DroV8525525.jpg?_i=_nF75D98DAEBA4CF2B502564351699CD99 159w" sizes="159px" />
</div>
<div itemprop="articleBody">
<co:body xmlns:co="www1.chabadonline.com/alpha1" xmlns:msxsl="urn:schemas-microsoft-com:xslt" xmlns:user="urn:my-scripts">
<div class="co_body article-body cf">
<p class="myth-green"><strong>Our Mission:</strong></p>
<p><span class="glossary_item" glossary_item="26003">Tzivos Hashem</span>: Jewish Children International is the foremost worldwide organization serving the physical and spiritual needs of Jewish children. Participants in <a href="/therebbe/livingtorah/player_cdo/aid/318994/jewish/Tzivos-Hashem-G-ds-Army-An-Inaugural-Speech.htm" title="Tzivos Hashem – G-d’s Army – An Inaugural Speech">Tzivos Hashem</a> programs are youngsters under the age of Bar/<span class="glossary_item" glossary_item="27884">Bat Mitzvah</span> from backgrounds spanning the spectrum of levels of Jewish education and commitment to Jewish affiliation, without regard to social and economic status.</p>
<p>From its headquarters in Brooklyn, Tzivos <span class="glossary_item" glossary_item="32524">Hashem</span> spearheads the trend to revive Jewish identity in children and provide them with a Jewish education through informal and entertaining programs, modern cutting edge teaching methods, first-class publications and personal encounters.</p>
<p>Enrollment in Tzivos <a href="/library/article_cdo/aid/433240/jewish/God.htm" title="G-d According to the Jews">Hashem</a> and following its program of increasing in <span class="glossary_item" glossary_item="33377">Torah</span> study and performance of <span class="glossary_item" glossary_item="31740">Mitzvos</span>, prepares today’s children for a seamless transition into Jewish adulthood, ensuring continuity of time-honored Jewish values and traditions.</p>
<p class="myth-green"><strong>Our Founder:</strong></p>
<div align="Left" class="imagetable left" width="91" style="PADDING-RIGHT: 5px">
<img src="https://w2.chabad.org/media/images/68/OXYl681405.jpg?_i=_nA2BB8AF97FCAED5F2987DA88AD756C4D" srcset="https://w2.chabad.org/media/images/68/OXYl681405.jpg?_i=_nA2BB8AF97FCAED5F2987DA88AD756C4D 91w" sizes="91px" loading="lazy" />
</div>
<p>World leader, <a href="/rebbe">Rabbi Menachem Mendel Schneerson, the Lubavitcher Rebbe</a>, of righteous memory, was sought after by top political figures, successful business people and the finest professionals for his sage advice on matters of grave importance. He was mentor and spiritual leader to hundreds of thousands of everyday people in all corners of the globe, no one was turned away. Yet, amidst his awesome schedule, the <span class="glossary_item" glossary_item="33607">Rebbe</span> busied himself with the lives of children, and set out to harness their great potential.</p>
<p>With a vision that has been unfolding and mushrooming for twenty years, the Rebbe called for the establishment of Tzivos Hashem in the fall of 1980. Children were a top priority for the Rebbe. Rather, each Jewish child was a top priority for the Rebbe. From his vantage point as world leader and spiritual giant, he understood the intrinsic promise held by children, and he founded Tzivos Hashem to cultivate and nurture them so that they could grow to be strong and healthy in body, mind and soul.</p>
<p>The Rebbe himself would hold communal meetings, which he called rallies, with thousands of children at a time. And it was the Rebbe himself who spoke to the children directly and put great responsibilities on their shoulders. Not only did the Rebbe see children as the promise of a better tomorrow, the Rebbe saw children as the promise for a better today.</p>
<p>Judaism stresses that chinuch, Jewish education, should begin at an early age to prepare for adulthood. The Rebbe emphasized that not only are children’s <a href="/library/article_cdo/aid/1438516/jewish/Mitzvah.htm" title="What Is a Mitzvah?">mitzvos</a> for the sake of practicing for the future, but that their mitzvos, now, while they are young, have significance in and of themselves. Through his confidence in them and his expectations, the Rebbe actually confirmed a child’s self esteem and challenged children to use their inborn strengths and talents for good.</p>
<p>The Tzivos Hashem relationship did not flow in just one direction, of commander to commandee. The soldiers of Tzivos Hashem gave <span class="glossary_item" glossary_item="33105">nachas</span> to the Rebbe as he watched them increase their mitzvos and perform them with greater care. And it was the children who were able to identify with and express the Rebbe’s passion to bring the world to peace and goodness, as they would sing for him their theme song: <span><strong>We Want <span class="glossary_item" glossary_item="30388">Moshiach</span> Now</strong></span></p>
</div>
</co:body>
</div>
<div class="break_floats"></div>
<div class="break_floats"></div>

<script type="text/javascript" src="https://w2.chabad.org/scripts/js/os/jquery-latest.min.js?v=63E55CA4"></script>
<script type="text/javascript" src="https://w2.chabad.org/scripts/js/os/jquery/jquery-noconflict.js?v=32FA5B68"></script>
<script type="text/javascript" src="https://w2.chabad.org/scripts/js/co/dist/CoLib.js?v=A241910E"></script>
<script type="text/javascript" src="https://w2.chabad.org/scripts/js/WebComponents/bundles/magen-cdo-global.js?v=68C37083"></script>
<script type="text/javascript" src="https://w2.chabad.org/scripts/js/templates/chabadorg/chabadorg.js?v=616FD2EA"></script>
<script type="text/javascript" src="https://w2.chabad.org/scripts/js/custom/multimedia/liveeventsbar.js?v=64A9602B"></script>
<script type="text/javascript" src="https://w2.chabad.org/scripts/js/custom/ChabadLocator.js?v=9193D1A8"></script>
<script type="text/javascript" src="https://w2.chabad.org/scripts/js/custom/BetaFeedback.js?v=5F3CBB58"></script>
<script type="text/javascript" src="https://w2.chabad.org/scripts/js/custom/deprecated.js?v=86975EC3"></script>
<script type="text/javascript" src="https://w2.chabad.org/scripts/js/OverrideJSDocumentWrite.js?v=9A0227AA"></script>
<script type="text/javascript" src="https://w2.chabad.org/scripts/js/custom/multimedia/infolayer.js?v=ED1B8531"></script>
<script type="text/javascript" src="https://w2.chabad.org/scripts/js/custom/commentsloader.js?v=0683C7A9"></script>

<script type="text/javascript" src="https://w2.chabad.org/scripts/js/custom/sitebanner.js?v=E560B55C"></script><script>$j = $j.fn ? $j : jQuery;$j(function(){$j.each($q,function(i,f){try{f.call(window);}catch(ex){console.error(ex);}});})</script>
<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript" src="https://w2.chabad.org/scripts/js/os/jquery-latest.min.js"></script>
<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
$j = jQuery.noConflict(); //prevent conflict with prototype, mootools javascript libraries
var cssNeeded = true;
var link, script;
var localNavigationJsNeeded = true;
var local_navigation_visible = false, closeEventAdded = false;
Co.DomEvents.AddListener(window, "domload", function ()
{
if (typeof (KidsSfx) == "undefined")
{
KidsSfx =
{
Sounds:
{
"sound1": null,
"sound2": null,
"sound3": null,
"sound4": null,
"sound5": null
}
};
KidsSfx.Initialize = function ()
{
for (var s in this.Sounds)
{
var sound = document.getElementById(s);
if (sound != null)
this.Sounds[s] = sound;
}
};
KidsSfx.PlaySound = function (InstanceId)
{
if (typeof (InstanceId) != "undefined" && typeof (this.Sounds[InstanceId]) != "undefined")
{
this.Sounds[InstanceId].currentTime = 0;
this.Sounds[InstanceId].volume = 0.1;
if (typeof (this.Sounds[InstanceId].play) != "undefined") {
this.Sounds[InstanceId].play();
}
return true;
}
return false;
};
KidsSfx.Initialize();
Co.Events.GlobalEvents.AddEventListener("kidssfx_playsound", KidsSfx.PlaySound, KidsSfx);
}
toggleNavigation();
Co.DomEvents.AddListener(window, 'resize', function ()
{
toggleNavigation();
});
$j('#header_container #logo.topBarLink a').click(function ()
{
window.location.href = '/kids/default.asp';
return false;
});
$j('#header_container #logo.topBarLink a img').css('display', 'none');
$j('#header_container #logo.topBarLink a').css('display', 'block');
$j('#header_container #logo.topBarLink a').css('height', '45px'); 
});
function toggleNavigation()
{
var size = Co.Tools.GetViewPaneSize();
var orientation = "";
if (size.Height > size.Width)
orientation = "portrait";
else if (size.Width > size.Height)
orientation = "landscape";
var mobileView = false;
if (orientation == "portrait")
mobileView = size.Width <= 768;
else if (orientation == "landscape")
mobileView = size.Width <= 1023;
if( !mobileView && Co.BrowserInfo.IsMobileDevice() )
{
mobileView = true;
cssNeeded = false;
}
if (mobileView)
{ 
if (localNavigationJsNeeded)
{
localNavigationJsNeeded = false;
//if ($j('.co_local_menu').length)
//{
// $j('#BodyContainer').css('marginTop', '3px');
// $j('#BodyContainer .body_wrapper').css('paddingTop', '0');
//}
$j(".co_local_menu").addClass("clearfix no_left_margin");
$j(".co_local_menu .body").css("position", "relative");
$j(".co_local_menu .body").append('<div class="bottom_close"><div class="background"></div></div>');
var height = $j(".co_local_menu .body").innerHeight();
$j(".co_local_menu .body").css("height", "0px");
$j(".co_local_menu .body").css("overflow", "hidden");
$j(".co_local_menu .header").addClass("close");
//toggle local navigtion on click of header
$j(".co_local_menu .header").click(function() {
toggleLocalNavigation($j(".co_local_menu .body"), local_navigation_visible, height);
return false;
});
}
if (cssNeeded)
{
cssNeeded = false;
link = document.createElement('link');
link.setAttribute("rel", "stylesheet");
link.setAttribute("type", "text/css");
link.href = '/css/mobile.css';
var links = document.getElementsByTagName('link');
var firstKidsLink = null;
for (var x = 0; x < links.length; x++)
{
var href = links[x].getAttribute('href');
if (href && href.indexOf('/kids') != -1)
{
firstKidsLink = links[x];
break;
}
}
if (firstKidsLink != null)
document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].insertBefore(link, firstKidsLink);
}
var navigation = Co.Tools.GetElementsByClassName('navigation', 'div', document.body)[0];
var button = document.getElementById('loginHeaderContainer');
if (navigation && button)
{
if (!Co.DomEvents.HasListener(button, 'click'))
{
Co.DomEvents.AddListener(button, 'click', function() {
if (document.body.className.indexOf('open') == -1)
Co.Tools.Content.AppendClassName(document.body, 'open');
else
Co.Tools.Content.RemoveClassName(document.body, 'open');
});
}
if (!Co.DomEvents.HasListener(document.getElementById('BodyContainer'), 'click'))
{
Co.DomEvents.AddListener(document.getElementById('BodyContainer'), 'click', function() {
if (document.body.className.indexOf('open') != -1)
Co.Tools.Content.RemoveClassName(document.body, 'open');
});
}
var footer = Co.Tools.GetElementsByClassName('footer_wrapper', 'DIV', document.body)[0];
if (!Co.DomEvents.HasListener(footer, 'click'))
{
Co.DomEvents.AddListener(footer, 'click', function() {
if (document.body.className.indexOf('open') != -1)
Co.Tools.Content.RemoveClassName(document.body, 'open');
});
}
}
}
else
{
if (typeof(link) != 'undefined' && link != null)
{
document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].removeChild(link);
cssNeeded = true;
if (!localNavigationJsNeeded)
{
//if ($j('.co_local_menu').length)
//{
// $j('#BodyContainer').css('marginTop', '5px');
// $j('#BodyContainer .body_wrapper').css('paddingTop', '15px');
//}
$j(".co_local_menu").removeClass("clearfix no_left_margin");
$j(".co_local_menu .body").css("position", "relative");
$j(".co_local_menu .body .bottom_close").remove();
$j(".co_local_menu .body").css("height", "auto");
$j(".co_local_menu .body").css("overflow", "auto");
$j(".co_local_menu .header").removeClass("close");
$j(".co_local_menu .header").removeClass("open");
$j(".co_local_menu .body").css("display", "block");
}
localNavigationJsNeeded = true;
}
}
}
//toggle local navigtion
function toggleLocalNavigation(obj, isVisible, height)
{
if (!isVisible)
{
if ($j(obj).css("display") == "none")
$j(obj).css("display", "block");
$j(obj).animate({ height: (height + 2) }, 200, function ()
{
local_navigation_visible = true;
$j(".co_local_menu .header").removeClass("close");
$j(".co_local_menu .header").addClass("open");
$j(".co_local_menu .body .bottom_close").css("display", "block");
if (!closeEventAdded)
{
$j(".co_local_menu .body .bottom_close").click(function ()
{
toggleLocalNavigation($j(".co_local_menu .body"), true, 0);
});
closeEventAdded = true;
}
});
}
else
{
$j(".co_local_menu .body .bottom_close").css("display", "none");
$j(obj).animate({ height: 0 }, 200, function ()
{
$j(".co_local_menu .header").removeClass("open");
$j(".co_local_menu .header").addClass("close");
local_navigation_visible = false;
});
}
}
</script>
